<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verwittigen.html>verwittigen</a> (14582)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to inform, to notify</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>More commonly used in the southern Dutch-speaking areas, especially Flanders, but universally understood. The more commonly used synonym in northern Netherlands and elsewhere <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:informeren.html>informeren</a></i>.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verwoesten.html>verwoesten</a> (6832)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woest.html>woest</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">inhospitable, desolate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woest.html>woest</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">woesten</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to destroy, waste, plunder</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***verzanden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verzanden.html>verzanden</a> (111390)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">versanden</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zand.html>zand</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verzanden.html>verzanden</a></strong>
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verzet.html>verzet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verzetje.html>verzetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">resistance</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">foreign occupation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> resistance <span class="Latn" lang="en">movement</span></li>
<li>(only in the diminutive) a <span class="Latn" lang="en">diversion</span>, an activity that distracts the mind.</li></ol>

***verzetten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verzetten.html>verzetten</a> (4947)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zetten.html>zetten</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verzetten.html>verzetten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to move, to shift to another position
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:verzette.html>verzette</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afspraak.html>afspraak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dokter.html>dokter</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>He <b>moved</b> his appointment with the doctor.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to perform, to do
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vandaag.html>vandaag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:verzet.html>verzet</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>He <b><a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a></b> a lot of work today.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:verzetten.html>verzetten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to resist</li></ol>

***verzinsel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verzinsel.html>verzinsel</a> (17093)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verzin.html>verzin</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verzinnen.html>verzinnen</a></i></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-sel</i>.
</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verzoeken.html>verzoeken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to tempt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> temptation

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verzorgd.html>verzorgd</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verzorgd.html>verzorgder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">verzorgdst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>careful, tidy, cultivated</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zwak.html>zwak</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.

</p>

***vestigen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vestigen.html>vestigen</a> (10011)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vestigen.html>vestigen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*festigon</i>, from an adjective <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*festig</i>. Replaced older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vesten.html>vesten</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vestigen.html>vestigen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to establish, to place</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to establish oneself</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to settle</li></ol>
